<response>None< /response>< Review>
There are many proud owner/operator garage door companies who invest in customer satisfaction by keeping it simple.  You can see them on the road in San Diego county all the time.  And most of them have excellent reviews.  They aren't the biggest options out there but really don't need to be at the same time.  These are your neighbors making a life for themselves.  They have maybe 1 or 2 company vehicles and only a few employees at best.  You often get a little lower price and a quicker install date.  They won't always offer the difficult custom stuff but at least stick with what they do best.  Offer garage door sales and service.  Invest in the vehicle they use to show company pride, up keeping vehicle(s) for safety and in the transportation of your purchased product(s).  Great recipe for success and your helping a local small business.
Gdu, however,  has too many products they offer and maybe even debt as one can see.  From  unsafe workspaces, vehicle upkeep, operational procedure, & general precautions abandoned.  The owner may need to choose 1 or 2 products only to offer and focus on safety.  Really start over with what worked 20yrs ago as the GDU heyday could have passed and appears to be in a little bit of trouble.
5 star ratings won't keep the customers / employees safe or pay your bills..< /Review>
